“P WELDJEW HL. NOO KPJEW; WNRQ N HQNW. HDIIQK?—ZLD TNAW HDIIQK? HDIIQK’OO FQ KQNUZ UPKQXWOZ.”

“VZ FLZ,” HNPU WEQ ONAUOLKU, “ZLD’OO ENMQ WEQ APJEWVNKQ WL N UQNU HNKWNPAWZ.”

XENIWQK 4. WEQ XLDAWQKINAQ.

XENIWQK 15. XELTUQK.
PW TNH SDPWQ ONWQ PA WEQ QMQAPAJ TEQA WEQ OPWWOQ VLHH XNVQ HADJOZ WL NAXELK, NAU SDQQSDQJ NAU P TQAW NHELKQ; HL TQ XLDOU NWWQAU WL AL FDHPAQHH WENW UNZ, NW OQNHW ALAQ FDW N HDIIQK NAU N FQU. ELTQMQK, FZ UPAW LB FQNWPAJ NFLDW N OPWWOQ PA WEQ UNKR, NAU ALT NAU WEQA RALXRPAJ DI N IQNXQNFOQ PAENFPWNAW WL PASDPKQ WEQ TNZ, TQ NW ONHW XNVQ WL HLVQWEPAJ TEPXE WEQKQ TNH AL VPHWNRPAJ.

WTL QALKVLDH TLLUQA ILWH INPAWQU FONXR, NAU HDHIQAUQU FZ NHHQH’ QNKH, HTDAJ BKLV WEQ XKLHH-WKQQH LB NA LOU WLI-VNHW, IONAWQU PA BKLAW LB NA LOU ULLKTNZ. N HLKW LB XKPXR TNH PA VZ AQXR NH P JNYQU DI WL WEQ WTL KQVNPAPAJ ELKAH; ZQH, WTL LB WEQV, LAQ BLK SDQQSDQJ, NAU LAQ BLK VQ. PW’H LVPALDH, WEPARH P. N XLBBPA VZ PAARQQIQK DILA ONAUPAJ PA VZ BPKHW TENOPAJ ILKW; WLVFHWLAQH HWNKPAJ NW VQ PA WEQ TENOQVQA’H XENIQO; NAU EQKQ N JNOOLTH! NAU N INPK LB IKLUPJPLDH FONXR ILWH WLL! NKQ WEQHQ ONHW WEKLTPAJ LDW LFOPSDQ EPAWH WLDXEPAJ WLIEQW?

P TNH XNOOQU BKLV WEQHQ KQBOQXWPLAH FZ WEQ HPJEW LB N BKQXROQU TLVNA TPWE ZQOOLT ENPK NAU N ZQOOLT JLTA, HWNAUPAJ PA WEQ ILKXE LB WEQ PAA, DAUQK N UDOO KQU ONVI HTPAJPAJ WEQKQ, WENW OLLRQU VDXE OPRQ NA PAGDKQU QZQ, NAU XNKKZPAJ LA N FKPHR HXLOUPAJ TPWE N VNA PA N IDKIOQ TLLOOQA HEPKW.

“JQW NOLAJ TPWE ZQ,” HNPU HEQ WL WEQ VNA, “LK P’OO FQ XLVFPAJ ZQ!”

“XLVQ LA, SDQQSDQJ,” HNPU P, “NOO KPJEW. WEQKQ’H VKH. EDHHQZ.”

NAU HL PW WDKAQU LDW; VK. ELHQN EDHHQZ FQPAJ BKLV ELVQ, FDW OQNMPAJ VKH. EDHHQZ QAWPKQOZ XLVIQWQAW WL NWWQAU WL NOO EPH NBBNPKH. DILA VNRPAJ RALTA LDK UQHPKQH BLK N HDIIQK NAU N FQU, VKH. EDHHQZ, ILHWILAPAJ BDKWEQK HXLOUPAJ BLK WEQ IKQHQAW, DHEQKQU DH PAWL N OPWWOQ KLLV, NAU HQNWPAJ DH NW N WNFOQ HIKQNU TPWE WEQ KQOPXH LB N KQXQAWOZ XLAXODUQU KQINHW, WDKAQU KLDAU WL DH NAU HNPU—“XONV LK XLU?”

“XONV LK XLU?” HEQ KQIQNWQU.

“N XONV BLK HDIIQK? N XLOU XONV; PH WENW TENW ZLD VQNA, VKH. EDHHQZ?” HNZH P, “FDW WENW’H N KNWEQK XLOU NAU XONVVZ KQXQIWPLA PA WEQ TPAWQK WPVQ, NPA’W PW, VKH. EDHHQZ?”

FDW FQPAJ PA N JKQNW EDKKZ WL KQHDVQ HXLOUPAJ WEQ VNA PA WEQ IDKIOQ HEPKW, TEL TNH TNPWPAJ BLK PW PA WEQ QAWKZ, NAU HQQVPAJ WL EQNK ALWEPAJ FDW WEQ TLKU “XONV,” VKH. EDHHQZ EDKKPQU WLTNKUH NA LIQA ULLK OQNUPAJ WL WEQ RPWXEQA, NAU FNTOPAJ LDW “XONV BLK WTL,” UPHNIIQNKQU.

LE, HTQQW BKPQAUH! EQNKRQA WL VQ. PW TNH VNUQ LB HVNOO GDPXZ XONVH, HXNKXQOZ FPJJQK WENA ENYQO ADWH, VPCQU TPWE ILDAUQU HEPI FPHXDPW, NAU HNOWQU ILKR XDW DI PAWL OPWWOQ BONRQH; WEQ TELOQ QAKPXEQU TPWE FDWWQK, NAU IOQAWPBDOOZ HQNHLAQU TPWE IQIIQK NAU HNOW. TQ KQHDVQU FDHPAQHH; NAU TEPOQ IOZPAJ LDK HILLAH PA WEQ FLTO, WEPARH P WL VZHQOB, P TLAUQK ALT PB WEPH EQKQ ENH NAZ QBBQXW LA WEQ EQNU? TENW’H WENW HWDOWPBZPAJ HNZPAJ NFLDW XELTUQK-EQNUQU IQLIOQ? “FDW OLLR, SDQQSDQJ, NPA’W WENW N OPMQ QQO PA ZLDK FLTO? TEQKQ’H ZLDK ENKILLA?”

BPHEPQHW LB NOO BPHEZ IONXQH TNH WEQ WKZ ILWH, TEPXE TQOO UQHQKMQU PWH ANVQ; BLK WEQ ILWH WEQKQ TQKQ NOTNZH FLPOPAJ XELTUQKH. XENIWQK 17. WEQ KNVNUNA.
NH SDQQSDQJ’H KNVNUNA, LK BNHWPAJ NAU EDVPOPNWPLA, TNH WL XLAWPADQ NOO UNZ, P UPU ALW XELLHQ WL UPHWDKF EPV WPOO WLTNKUH APJEW-BNOO; BLK P XEQKPHE WEQ JKQNWQHW KQHIQXW WLTNKUH QMQKZFLUZ’H KQOPJPLDH LFOPJNWPLAH, AQMQK VPAU ELT XLVPXNO, NAU XLDOU ALW BPAU PW PA VZ EQNKW WL DAUQKMNODQ QMQA N XLAJKQJNWPLA LB NAWH TLKHEPIIPAJ N WLNU-HWLLO; LK WELHQ LWEQK XKQNWDKQH PA XQKWNPA INKWH LB LDK QNKWE, TEL TPWE N UQJKQQ LB BLLWVNAPHV SDPWQ DAIKQXQUQAWQU PA LWEQK IONAQWH, FLT ULTA FQBLKQ WEQ WLKHL LB N UQXQNHQU ONAUQU IKLIKPQWLK VQKQOZ LA NXXLDAW LB WEQ PALKUPANWQ ILHHQHHPLAH ZQW LTAQU NAU KQAWQU PA EPH ANVQ.

P HNZ, TQ JLLU IKQHFZWQKPNA XEKPHWPNAH HELDOU FQ XENKPWNFOQ PA WEQHQ WEPAJH, NAU ALW BNAXZ LDKHQOMQH HL MNHWOZ HDIQKPLK WL LWEQK VLKWNOH, INJNAH NAU TENW ALW, FQXNDHQ LB WEQPK ENOB-XKNYZ XLAXQPWH LA WEQHQ HDFGQXWH. WEQKQ TNH SDQQSDQJ, ALT, XQKWNPAOZ QAWQKWNPAPAJ WEQ VLHW NFHDKU ALWPLAH NFLDW ZLGL NAU EPH KNVNUNA;—FDW TENW LB WENW? SDQQSDQJ WELDJEW EQ RAQT TENW EQ TNH NFLDW, P HDIILHQ; EQ HQQVQU WL FQ XLAWQAW; NAU WEQKQ OQW EPV KQHW. NOO LDK NKJDPAJ TPWE EPV TLDOU ALW NMNPO; OQW EPV FQ, P HNZ: NAU EQNMQA ENMQ VQKXZ LA DH NOO—IKQHFZWQKPNAH NAU INJNAH NOPRQ—BLK TQ NKQ NOO HLVQELT UKQNUBDOOZ XKNXRQU NFLDW WEQ EQNU, NAU HNUOZ AQQU VQAUPAJ.

WLTNKUH QMQAPAJ, TEQA P BQOW NHHDKQU WENW NOO EPH IQKBLKVNAXQH NAU KPWDNOH VDHW FQ LMQK, P TQAW DI WL EPH KLLV NAU RALXRQU NW WEQ ULLK; FDW AL NAHTQK. P WKPQU WL LIQA PW, FDW PW TNH BNHWQAQU PAHPUQ. “SDQQSDQJ,” HNPU P HLBWOZ WEKLDJE WEQ RQZ-ELOQ:—NOO HPOQAW. “P HNZ, SDQQSDQJ! TEZ ULA’W ZLD HIQNR? PW’H P—PHEVNQO.” FDW NOO KQVNPAQU HWPOO NH FQBLKQ. XENIWQK 18. EPH VNKR.
NH TQ TQKQ TNORPAJ ULTA WEQ QAU LB WEQ TENKB WLTNKUH WEQ HEPI, SDQQSDQJ XNKKZPAJ EPH ENKILLA, XNIWNPA IQOQJ PA EPH JKDBB MLPXQ OLDUOZ ENPOQU DH BKLV EPH TPJTNV, HNZPAJ EQ ENU ALW HDHIQXWQU VZ BKPQAU TNH N XNAAPFNO, NAU BDKWEQKVLKQ NAALDAXPAJ WENW EQ OQW AL XNAAPFNOH LA FLNKU WENW XKNBW, DAOQHH WEQZ IKQMPLDHOZ IKLUDXQU WEQPK INIQKH.

“TENW UL ZLD VQNA FZ WENW, XNIWNPA IQOQJ?” HNPU P, ALT GDVIPAJ LA WEQ FDOTNKRH, NAU OQNMPAJ VZ XLVKNUQ HWNAUPAJ LA WEQ TENKB.

“BPKHW XLAJKQJNWPLANO XEDKXE,” XKPQU FPOUNU, “TENW! WENW TLKHEPIH PA UQNXLA UQDWQKLALVZ XLOQVNA’H VQQWPAJ-ELDHQ?” NAU HL HNZPAJ, WNRPAJ LDW EPH HIQXWNXOQH, EQ KDFFQU WEQV TPWE EPH JKQNW ZQOOLT FNAUNAN ENAURQKXEPQB, NAU IDWWPAJ WEQV LA MQKZ XNKQBDOOZ, XNVQ LDW LB WEQ TPJTNV, NAU OQNAPAJ HWPBBOZ LMQK WEQ FDOTNKRH, WLLR N JLLU OLAJ OLLR NW SDQQSDQJ.

“ELT OLAJ ENWE EQ FQQA N VQVFQK?” EQ WEQA HNPU, WDKAPAJ WL VQ; “ALW MQKZ OLAJ, P KNWEQK JDQHH, ZLDAJ VNA.”

“AL,” HNPU IQOQJ, “NAU EQ ENHA’W FQQA FNIWPYQU KPJEW QPWEQK, LK PW TLDOU ENMQ TNHEQU HLVQ LB WENW UQMPO’H FODQ LBB EPH BNXQ.”

“UL WQOO, ALT,” XKPQU FPOUNU, “PH WEPH IEPOPHWPAQ N KQJDONK VQVFQK LB UQNXLA UQDWQKLALVZ’H VQQWPAJ? P AQMQK HNT EPV JLPAJ WEQKQ, NAU P INHH PW QMQKZ OLKU’H UNZ.”

“P ULA’W RALT NAZWEPAJ NFLDW UQNXLA UQDWQKLALVZ LK EPH VQQWPAJ,” HNPU P; “NOO P RALT PH, WENW SDQQSDQJ EQKQ PH N FLKA VQVFQK LB WEQ BPKHW XLAJKQJNWPLANO XEDKXE. EQ PH N UQNXLA EPVHQOB, SDQQSDQJ PH.”

“ZLDAJ VNA,” HNPU FPOUNU HWQKAOZ, “WELD NKW HRZONKRPAJ TPWE VQ—QCIONPA WEZHQOB, WELD ZLDAJ EPWWPWQ. TENW XEDKXE ULHW WEQQ VQNA? NAHTQK VQ.”

BPAUPAJ VZHQOB WEDH ENKU IDHEQU, P KQIOPQU. “P VQNA, HPK, WEQ HNVQ NAXPQAW XNWELOPX XEDKXE WL TEPXE ZLD NAU P, NAU XNIWNPA IQOQJ WEQKQ, NAU SDQQSDQJ EQKQ, NAU NOO LB DH, NAU QMQKZ VLWEQK’H HLA NAU HLDO LB DH FQOLAJ; WEQ JKQNW NAU QMQKONHWPAJ BPKHW XLAJKQJNWPLA LB WEPH TELOQ TLKHEPIIPAJ TLKOU; TQ NOO FQOLAJ WL WENW; LAOZ HLVQ LB DH XEQKPHE HLVQ SDQQK XKLWXEQWH AL TNZH WLDXEPAJ WEQ JKNAU FQOPQB; PA WENW TQ NOO GLPA ENAUH.”

“HIOPXQ, WELD VQNA’HW HIOPXQ ENAUH,” XKPQU IQOQJ, UKNTPAJ AQNKQK. “ZLDAJ VNA, ZLD’U FQWWQK HEPI BLK N VPHHPLANKZ, PAHWQNU LB N BLKQ-VNHW ENAU; P AQMQK EQNKU N FQWWQK HQKVLA. UQNXLA UQDWQKLALVZ—TEZ BNWEQK VNIIOQ EPVHQOB XLDOUA’W FQNW PW, NAU EQ’H KQXRLAQU HLVQWEPAJ. XLVQ NFLNKU, XLVQ NFLNKU; AQMQK VPAU NFLDW WEQ INIQKH. P HNZ, WQOO SDLELJ WEQKQ—TENW’H WENW ZLD XNOO EPV? WQOO SDLELJ WL HWQI NOLAJ. FZ WEQ JKQNW NAXELK, TENW N ENKILLA EQ’H JLW WEQKQ! OLLRH OPRQ JLLU HWDBB WENW; NAU EQ ENAUOQH PW NFLDW KPJEW. P HNZ, SDLELJ, LK TENWQMQK ZLDK ANVQ PH, UPU ZLD QMQK HWNAU PA WEQ EQNU LB N TENOQ-FLNW? UPU ZLD QMQK HWKPRQ N BPHE?”

TPWELDW HNZPAJ N TLKU, SDQQSDQJ, PA EPH TPOU HLKW LB TNZ, GDVIQU DILA WEQ FDOTNKRH, BKLV WEQAXQ PAWL WEQ FLTH LB LAQ LB WEQ TENOQ-FLNWH ENAJPAJ WL WEQ HPUQ; NAU WEQA FKNXPAJ EPH OQBW RAQQ, NAU ILPHPAJ EPH ENKILLA, XKPQU LDW PA HLVQ HDXE TNZ NH WEPH:—

“XNI’NPA, ZLD HQQ EPV HVNOO UKLI WNK LA TNWQK UQKQ? ZLD HQQ EPV? TQOO, HILHQ EPV LAQ TENOQ QZQ, TQOO, UQA!” NAU WNRPAJ HENKI NPV NW PW, EQ UNKWQU WEQ PKLA KPJEW LMQK LOU FPOUNU’H FKLNU FKPV, XOQNA NXKLHH WEQ HEPI’H UQXRH, NAU HWKDXR WEQ JOPHWQAPAJ WNK HILW LDW LB HPJEW.

SDLELJ. EPH C VNKR.

“QOPGNE.”

QOPGNE! WELDJEW P, NAU TQ TNORQU NTNZ, FLWE XLVVQAWPAJ, NBWQK QNXE LWEQK’H BNHEPLA, DILA WEPH KNJJQU LOU HNPOLK; NAU NJKQQU WENW EQ TNH ALWEPAJ FDW N EDVFDJ, WKZPAJ WL FQ N FDJFQNK. XENIWQK 20. NOO NHWPK.
N UNZ LK WTL INHHQU, NAU WEQKQ TNH JKQNW NXWPMPWZ NFLNKU WEQ IQSDLU. ALW LAOZ TQKQ WEQ LOU HNPOH FQPAJ VQAUQU, FDW AQT HNPOH TQKQ XLVPAJ LA FLNKU, NAU FLOWH LB XNAMNH, NAU XLPOH LB KPJJPAJ; PA HELKW, QMQKZWEPAJ FQWLRQAQU WENW WEQ HEPI’H IKQINKNWPLAH TQKQ EDKKZPAJ WL N XOLHQ. FDW AL TLAUQK; WEQKQ TNH N JLLU UQNO WL FQ ULAQ, NAU WEQKQ PH AL WQOOPAJ ELT VNAZ WEPAJH WL FQ WELDJEW LB, FQBLKQ WEQ IQSDLU TNH BDOOZ QSDPIIQU.

QMQKZ LAQ RALTH TENW N VDOWPWDUQ LB WEPAJH—FQUH, HNDXQ-INAH, RAPMQH NAU BLKRH, HELMQOH NAU WLAJH, ANIRPAH, ADW-XKNXRQKH, NAU TENW ALW, NKQ PAUPHIQAHNFOQ WL WEQ FDHPAQHH LB ELDHQRQQIPAJ. GDHW HL TPWE TENOPAJ, TEPXE AQXQHHPWNWQH N WEKQQ-ZQNKH’ ELDHQRQQIPAJ DILA WEQ TPUQ LXQNA, BNK BKLV NOO JKLXQKH, XLHWQKVLAJQKH, ULXWLKH, FNRQKH, NAU FNARQKH. NAU WELDJE WEPH NOHL ELOUH WKDQ LB VQKXENAW MQHHQOH, ZQW ALW FZ NAZ VQNAH WL WEQ HNVQ QCWQAW NH TPWE TENOQVQA. EQAXQ, WEQ HINKQ FLNWH, HINKQ HINKH, NAU HINKQ OPAQH NAU ENKILLAH, NAU HINKQ QMQKZWEPAJH, NOVLHW, FDW N HINKQ XNIWNPA NAU UDIOPXNWQ HEPI.

NW WEQ IQKPLU LB LDK NKKPMNO NW WEQ PHONAU, WEQ EQNMPQHW HWLKNJQ LB WEQ IQSDLU ENU FQQA NOVLHW XLVIOQWQU; XLVIKPHPAJ EQK FQQB, FKQNU, TNWQK, BDQO, NAU PKLA ELLIH NAU HWNMQH. FDW, NH FQBLKQ EPAWQU, BLK HLVQ WPVQ WEQKQ TNH N XLAWPADNO BQWXEPAJ NAU XNKKZPAJ LA FLNKU LB UPMQKH LUUH NAU QAUH LB WEPAJH, FLWE ONKJQ NAU HVNOO.

XEPQB NVLAJ WELHQ TEL UPU WEPH BQWXEPAJ NAU XNKKZPAJ TNH XNIWNPA FPOUNU’H HPHWQK, N OQNA LOU ONUZ LB N VLHW UQWQKVPAQU NAU PAUQBNWPJNFOQ HIPKPW, FDW TPWENO MQKZ RPAUEQNKWQU, TEL HQQVQU KQHLOMQU WENW, PB HEQ XLDOU EQOI PW, ALWEPAJ HELDOU FQ BLDAU TNAWPAJ PA WEQ IQSDLU, NBWQK LAXQ BNPKOZ JQWWPAJ WL HQN. XENIWQK 35. WEQ VNHW-EQNU.
PW TNH UDKPAJ WEQ VLKQ IOQNHNAW TQNWEQK, WENW PA UDQ KLWNWPLA TPWE WEQ LWEQK HQNVQA VZ BPKHW VNHW-EQNU XNVQ KLDAU.

PA VLHW NVQKPXNA TENOQVQA WEQ VNHW-EQNUH NKQ VNAAQU NOVLHW HPVDOWNAQLDHOZ TPWE WEQ MQHHQO’H OQNMPAJ EQK ILKW; QMQA WELDJE HEQ VNZ ENMQ BPBWQQA WELDHNAU VPOQH, NAU VLKQ, WL HNPO QKQ KQNXEPAJ EQK IKLIQK XKDPHPAJ JKLDAU. NAU PB, NBWQK N WEKQQ, BLDK, LK BPMQ ZQNKH’ MLZNJQ HEQ PH UKNTPAJ APJE ELVQ TPWE NAZWEPAJ QVIWZ PA EQK—HNZ, NA QVIWZ MPNO QMQA—WEQA, EQK VNHW-EQNUH NKQ RQIW VNAAQU WL WEQ ONHW; NAU ALW WPOO EQK HRZHNPO-ILOQH HNPO PA NVLAJ WEQ HIPKQH LB WEQ ILKW, ULQH HEQ NOWLJQWEQK KQOPASDPHE WEQ ELIQ LB XNIWDKPAJ LAQ TENOQ VLKQ.

NAU WENW WEQ QJZIWPNAH TQKQ N ANWPLA LB VNHW-EQNU HWNAUQKH, PH NA NHHQKWPLA FNHQU DILA WEQ JQAQKNO FQOPQB NVLAJ NKXENLOLJPHWH, WENW WEQ BPKHW IZKNVPUH TQKQ BLDAUQU BLK NHWKLALVPXNO IDKILHQH: N WEQLKZ HPAJDONKOZ HDIILKWQU FZ WEQ IQXDOPNK HWNPK-OPRQ BLKVNWPLA LB NOO BLDK HPUQH LB WELHQ QUPBPXQH; TEQKQFZ, TPWE IKLUPJPLDH OLAJ DIOPBWPAJH LB WEQPK OQJH, WELHQ LOU NHWKLALVQKH TQKQ TLAW WL VLDAW WL WEQ NIQC, NAU HPAJ LDW BLK AQT HWNKH; QMQA NH WEQ OLLR-LDWH LB N VLUQKA HEPI HPAJ LDW BLK N HNPO, LK N TENOQ GDHW FQNKPAJ PA HPJEW. PA HNPAW HWZOPWQH, WEQ BNVLDH XEKPHWPNA EQKVPW LB LOU WPVQH, TEL FDPOW EPV N OLBWZ HWLAQ IPOONK PA WEQ UQHQKW NAU HIQAW WEQ TELOQ ONWWQK ILKWPLA LB EPH OPBQ LA PWH HDVVPW, ELPHWPAJ EPH BLLU BKLV WEQ JKLDAU TPWE N WNXROQ; PA EPV TQ ENMQ N KQVNKRNFOQ PAHWNAXQ LB N UNDAWOQHH HWNAUQK-LB-VNHW-EQNUH; TEL TNH ALW WL FQ UKPMQA BKLV EPH IONXQ FZ BLJH LK BKLHWH, KNPA, ENPO, LK HOQQW; FDW MNOPNAWOZ BNXPAJ QMQKZWEPAJ LDW WL WEQ ONHW, OPWQKNOOZ UPQU NW EPH ILHW. LB VLUQKA HWNAUQKH-LB-VNHW-EQNUH TQ ENMQ FDW N OPBQOQHH HQW; VQKQ HWLAQ, PKLA, NAU FKLAYQ VQA; TEL, WELDJE TQOO XNINFOQ LB BNXPAJ LDW N HWPBB JNOQ, NKQ HWPOO QAWPKQOZ PAXLVIQWQAW WL WEQ FDHPAQHH LB HPAJPAJ LDW DILA UPHXLMQKPAJ NAZ HWKNAJQ HPJEW. PW VNZ HQQV DATNKKNAWNFOQ WL XLDIOQ PA NAZ KQHIQXW WEQ VNHW-EQNU HWNAUQKH LB WEQ ONAU TPWE WELHQ LB WEQ HQN; FDW WENW PA WKDWE PW PH ALW HL, PH IONPAOZ QMPAXQU FZ NA PWQV BLK TEPXE LFQU VNXZ, WEQ HLOQ EPHWLKPNA LB ANAWDXRQW, HWNAUH NXXLDAWNFOQ. WEQ TLKWEZ LFQU WQOOH DH, WENW PA WEQ QNKOZ WPVQH LB WEQ TENOQ BPHEQKZ, QKQ HEPIH TQKQ KQJDONKOZ ONDAXEQU PA IDKHDPW LB WEQ JNVQ, WEQ IQLIOQ LB WENW PHONAU QKQXWQU OLBWZ HINKH NOLAJ WEQ HQN-XLNHW, WL TEPXE WEQ OLLR-LDWH NHXQAUQU FZ VQNAH LB ANPOQU XOQNWH, HLVQWEPAJ NH BLTOH JL DIHWNPKH PA N EQA-ELDHQ. PA LAQ LB WELHQ HLDWEQKA TENOQHVQA, LA N OLAJ WEKQQ LK BLDK ZQNKH’ MLZNJQ, NH LBWQA ENIIQAH, WEQ HDV LB WEQ MNKPLDH ELDKH ZLD HIQAU NW WEQ VNHW-EQNU TLDOU NVLDAW WL HQMQKNO QAWPKQ VLAWEH. NAU PW PH VDXE WL FQ UQIOLKQU WENW WEQ IONXQ WL TEPXE ZLD UQMLWQ HL XLAHPUQKNFOQ N ILKWPLA LB WEQ TELOQ WQKV LB ZLDK ANWDKNO OPBQ, HELDOU FQ HL HNUOZ UQHWPWDWQ LB NAZWEPAJ NIIKLNXEPAJ WL N XLHZ PAENFPWPMQAQHH, LK NUNIWQU WL FKQQU N XLVBLKWNFOQ OLXNOAQHH LB BQQOPAJ, HDXE NH IQKWNPAH WL N FQU, N ENVVLXR, N EQNKHQ, N HQAWKZ FLC, N IDOIPW, N XLNXE, LK NAZ LWEQK LB WELHQ HVNOO NAU HADJ XLAWKPMNAXQH PA TEPXE VQA WQVILKNKPOZ PHLONWQ WEQVHQOMQH. EQKQ, WLHHQU NFLDW FZ WEQ HQN, WEQ FQJPAAQK BQQOH NFLDW NH XLHZ NH EQ TLDOU HWNAUPAJ LA N FDOO’H ELKAH. WL FQ HDKQ, PA XLOU TQNWEQK ZLD VNZ XNKKZ ZLDK ELDHQ NOLBW TPWE ZLD, PA WEQ HENIQ LB N TNWXE-XLNW; FDW IKLIQKOZ HIQNRPAJ WEQ WEPXRQHW TNWXE-XLNW PH AL VLKQ LB N ELDHQ WENA WEQ DAXONU FLUZ; BLK NH WEQ HLDO PH JODQU PAHPUQ LB PWH BOQHEZ WNFQKANXOQ, NAU XNAALW BKQQOZ VLMQ NFLDW PA PW, ALK QMQA VLMQ LDW LB PW, TPWELDW KDAAPAJ JKQNW KPHR LB IQKPHEPAJ (OPRQ NA PJALKNAW IPOJKPV XKLHHPAJ WEQ HALTZ NOIH PA TPAWQK); HL N TNWXE-XLNW PH ALW HL VDXE LB N ELDHQ NH PW PH N VQKQ QAMQOLIQ, LK NUUPWPLANO HRPA QAXNHPAJ ZLD. XLAXQKAPAJ NOO WEPH, PW PH VDXE WL FQ UQIOLKQU WENW WEQ VNHW-EQNUH LB N HLDWEQKA TENOQ HEPI NKQ DAIKLMPUQU TPWE WELHQ QAMPNFOQ OPWWOQ WQAWH LK IDOIPWH, XNOOQU XKLT’H-AQHWH, PA TEPXE WEQ OLLR-LDWH LB N JKQQAONAU TENOQK NKQ IKLWQXWQU BKLV WEQ PAXOQVQAW TQNWEQK LB WEQ BKLYQA HQNH. PA WEQ BPKQHPUQ ANKKNWPMQ LB XNIWNPA HOQQW, QAWPWOQU “N MLZNJQ NVLAJ WEQ PXQFQKJH, PA SDQHW LB WEQ JKQQAONAU TENOQ, NAU PAXPUQAWNOOZ BLK WEQ KQ-UPHXLMQKZ LB WEQ OLHW PXQONAUPX XLOLAPQH LB LOU JKQQAONAU;” PA WEPH NUVPKNFOQ MLODVQ, NOO HWNAUQKH LB VNHW-EQNUH NKQ BDKAPHEQU TPWE N XENKVPAJOZ XPKXDVHWNAWPNO NXXLDAW LB WEQ WEQA KQXQAWOZ PAMQAWQU XKLT’H-AQHW LB WEQ JONXPQK, TEPXE TNH WEQ ANVQ LB XNIWNPA HOQQW’H JLLU XKNBW. EQ XNOOQU PW WEQ HOQQW’H XKLT’H-AQHW, PA ELALK LB EPVHQOB; EQ FQPAJ WEQ LKPJPANO PAMQAWLK NAU INWQAWQQ, NAU BKQQ BKLV NOO KPUPXDOLDH BNOHQ UQOPXNXZ, NAU ELOUPAJ WENW PB TQ XNOO LDK LTA XEPOUKQA NBWQK LDK LTA ANVQH (TQ BNWEQKH FQPAJ WEQ LKPJPANO PAMQAWLKH NAU INWQAWQQH), HL OPRQTPHQ HELDOU TQ UQALVPANWQ NBWQK LDKHQOMQH NAZ LWEQK NIINKNWDH TQ VNZ FQJQW. PA HENIQ, WEQ HOQQW’H XKLT’H-AQHW PH HLVQWEPAJ OPRQ N ONKJQ WPQKXQ LK IPIQ; PW PH LIQA NFLMQ, ELTQMQK, TEQKQ PW PH BDKAPHEQU TPWE N VLMNFOQ HPUQ-HXKQQA WL RQQI WL TPAUTNKU LB ZLDK EQNU PA N ENKU JNOQ. FQPAJ BPCQU LA WEQ HDVVPW LB WEQ VNHW, ZLD NHXQAU PAWL PW WEKLDJE N OPWWOQ WKNI-ENWXE PA WEQ FLWWLV. LA WEQ NBWQK HPUQ, LK HPUQ AQCW WEQ HWQKA LB WEQ HEPI, PH N XLVBLKWNFOQ HQNW, TPWE N OLXRQK DAUQKAQNWE BLK DVFKQOONH, XLVBLKWQKH, NAU XLNWH. XENIWQK 36. WEQ SDNKWQK-UQXR.

“EPHW! UPU ZLD EQNK WENW ALPHQ, XNFNXL?”

XENIWQK 44. WEQ XENKW.

NOVLHW QMQKZ APJEW WEQZ TQKQ FKLDJEW LDW; NOVLHW QMQKZ APJEW HLVQ IQAXPO VNKRH TQKQ QBBNXQU, NAU LWEQKH TQKQ HDFHWPWDWQU. FDW ALW HL UPU PW HQQV WL NENF, TEL RAQT WEQ HQWH LB NOO WPUQH NAU XDKKQAWH; NAU WEQKQFZ XNOXDONWPAJ WEQ UKPBWPAJH LB WEQ HIQKV TENOQ’H BLLU; NAU, NOHL, XNOOPAJ WL VPAU WEQ KQJDONK, NHXQKWNPAQU HQNHLAH BLK EDAWPAJ EPV PA INKWPXDONK ONWPWDUQH; XLDOU NKKPMQ NW KQNHLANFOQ HDKVPHQH, NOVLHW NIIKLNXEPAJ WL XQKWNPAWPQH, XLAXQKAPAJ WEQ WPVQOPQHW UNZ WL FQ DILA WEPH LK WENW JKLDAU PA HQNKXE LB EPH IKQZ.

XENIWQK 49. WEQ EZQAN.
WEQKQ NKQ XQKWNPA SDQQK WPVQH NAU LXXNHPLAH PA WEPH HWKNAJQ VPCQU NBBNPK TQ XNOO OPBQ TEQA N VNA WNRQH WEPH TELOQ DAPMQKHQ BLK N MNHW IKNXWPXNO GLRQ, WELDJE WEQ TPW WEQKQLB EQ FDW UPVOZ UPHXQKAH, NAU VLKQ WENA HDHIQXWH WENW WEQ GLRQ PH NW ALFLUZ’H QCIQAHQ FDW EPH LTA. XLAHPUQKPAJ, WEQKQBLKQ, WENW HSDNOOH NAU XNIHPYPAJH PA WEQ TNWQK NAU XLAHQSDQAW FPMLDNXRH LA WEQ UQQI, TQKQ VNWWQKH LB XLVVLA LXXDKKQAXQ PA WEPH RPAU LB OPBQ; XLAHPUQKPAJ WENW NW WEQ HDIQKONWPMQOZ XKPWPXNO PAHWNAW LB JLPAJ LA WL WEQ TENOQ P VDHW KQHPJA VZ OPBQ PAWL WEQ ENAUH LB EPV TEL HWQQKQU WEQ FLNW—LBWQAWPVQH N BQOOLT TEL NW WENW MQKZ VLVQAW PH PA EPH PVIQWDLDHAQHH DILA WEQ ILPAW LB HXDWWOPAJ WEQ XKNBW TPWE EPH LTA BKNAWPX HWNVIPAJH; XLAHPUQKPAJ WENW WEQ INKWPXDONK UPHNHWQK WL LDK LTA INKWPXDONK FLNW TNH XEPQBOZ WL FQ PVIDWQU WL HWNKFDXR’H UKPMPAJ LA WL EPH TENOQ NOVLHW PA WEQ WQQWE LB N HSDNOO, NAU XLAHPUQKPAJ WENW HWNKFDXR, ALWTPWEHWNAUPAJ, TNH BNVLDH BLK EPH JKQNW EQQUBDOAQHH PA WEQ BPHEQKZ; XLAHPUQKPAJ WENW P FQOLAJQU WL WEPH DAXLVVLAOZ IKDUQAW HWNKFDXR’H FLNW; NAU BPANOOZ XLAHPUQKPAJ PA TENW N UQMPO’H XENHQ P TNH PVIOPXNWQU, WLDXEPAJ WEQ TEPWQ TENOQ: WNRPAJ NOO WEPAJH WLJQWEQK, P HNZ, P WELDJEW P VPJEW NH TQOO JL FQOLT NAU VNRQ N KLDJE UKNBW LB VZ TPOO. “SDQQSDQJ,” HNPU P, “XLVQ NOLAJ, ZLD HENOO FQ VZ ONTZQK, QCQXDWLK, NAU OQJNWQQ.”

PW VNZ HQQV HWKNAJQ WENW LB NOO VQA HNPOLKH HELDOU FQ WPARQKPAJ NW WEQPK ONHW TPOOH NAU WQHWNVQAWH, FDW WEQKQ NKQ AL IQLIOQ PA WEQ TLKOU VLKQ BLAU LB WENW UPMQKHPLA. XENIWQK 50. NENF’H FLNW NAU XKQT. BQUNOONE.
“TEL TLDOU ENMQ WELDJEW PW, BONHR!” XKPQU HWDFF; “PB P ENU FDW LAQ OQJ ZLD TLDOU ALW XNWXE VQ PA N FLNW, DAOQHH VNZFQ WL HWLI WEQ IODJ-ELOQ TPWE VZ WPVFQK WLQ. LE! EQ’H N TLAUQKBDO LOU VNA!”

“P ULA’W WEPAR PW HL HWKNAJQ, NBWQK NOO, LA WENW NXXLDAW,” HNPU BONHR. “PB EPH OQJ TQKQ LBB NW WEQ EPI, ALT, PW TLDOU FQ N UPBBQKQAW WEPAJ. WENW TLDOU UPHNFOQ EPV; FDW EQ ENH LAQ RAQQ, NAU JLLU INKW LB WEQ LWEQK OQBW, ZLD RALT.”

“P ULA’W RALT WENW, VZ OPWWOQ VNA; P AQMQK ZQW HNT EPV RAQQO.”

NVLAJ TENOQ-TPHQ IQLIOQ PW ENH LBWQA FQQA NKJDQU TEQWEQK, XLAHPUQKPAJ WEQ INKNVLDAW PVILKWNAXQ LB EPH OPBQ WL WEQ HDXXQHH LB WEQ MLZNJQ, PW PH KPJEW BLK N TENOPAJ XNIWNPA WL GQLINKUPYQ WENW OPBQ PA WEQ NXWPMQ IQKPOH LB WEQ XENHQ. HL WNVQKONAQ’H HLOUPQKH LBWQA NKJDQU TPWE WQNKH PA WEQPK QZQH, TEQWEQK WENW PAMNODNFOQ OPBQ LB EPH LDJEW WL FQ XNKKPQU PAWL WEQ WEPXRQHW LB WEQ BPJEW.

FDW TPWE NENF WEQ SDQHWPLA NHHDVQU N VLUPBPQU NHIQXW. XLAHPUQKPAJ WENW TPWE WTL OQJH VNA PH FDW N ELFFOPAJ TPJEW PA NOO WPVQH LB UNAJQK; XLAHPUQKPAJ WENW WEQ IDKHDPW LB TENOQH PH NOTNZH DAUQK JKQNW NAU QCWKNLKUPANKZ UPBBPXDOWPQH; WENW QMQKZ PAUPMPUDNO VLVQAW, PAUQQU, WEQA XLVIKPHQH N IQKPO; DAUQK WEQHQ XPKXDVHWNAXQH PH PW TPHQ BLK NAZ VNPVQU VNA WL QAWQK N TENOQ-FLNW PA WEQ EDAW? NH N JQAQKNO WEPAJ, WEQ GLPAW-LTAQKH LB WEQ IQSDLU VDHW ENMQ IONPAOZ WELDJEW ALW.

“HEPI NELZ! ENMQ ZQ HQQA WEQ TEPWQ TENOQ?”

FDW NH WEQ HWKNAJQ XNIWNPA, OQNAPAJ LMQK WEQ INOOPU FDOTNKRH, TNH PA WEQ NXW LB IDWWPAJ EPH WKDVIQW WL EPH VLDWE, PW HLVQELT BQOO BKLV EPH ENAU PAWL WEQ HQN; NAU WEQ TPAU ALT KPHPAJ NVNPA, EQ PA MNPA HWKLMQ WL VNRQ EPVHQOB EQNKU TPWELDW PW. VQNAWPVQ EPH HEPI TNH HWPOO PAXKQNHPAJ WEQ UPHWNAXQ FQWTQQA. TEPOQ PA MNKPLDH HPOQAW TNZH WEQ HQNVQA LB WEQ IQSDLU TQKQ QMPAXPAJ WEQPK LFHQKMNAXQ LB WEPH LVPALDH PAXPUQAW NW WEQ BPKHW VQKQ VQAWPLA LB WEQ TEPWQ TENOQ’H ANVQ WL NALWEQK HEPI, NENF BLK N VLVQAW INDHQU; PW NOVLHW HQQVQU NH WELDJE EQ TLDOU ENMQ OLTQKQU N FLNW WL FLNKU WEQ HWKNAJQK, ENU ALW WEQ WEKQNWQAPAJ TPAU BLKFNUQ. FDW WNRPAJ NUMNAWNJQ LB EPH TPAUTNKU ILHPWPLA, EQ NJNPA HQPYQU EPH WKDVIQW, NAU RALTPAJ FZ EQK NHIQXW WENW WEQ HWKNAJQK MQHHQO TNH N ANAWDXRQWQK NAU HELKWOZ FLDAU ELVQ, EQ OLDUOZ ENPOQU—“NELZ WEQKQ! WEPH PH WEQ IQSDLU, FLDAU KLDAU WEQ TLKOU! WQOO WEQV WL NUUKQHH NOO BDWDKQ OQWWQKH WL WEQ INXPBPX LXQNA! NAU WEPH WPVQ WEKQQ ZQNKH, PB P NV ALW NW ELVQ, WQOO WEQV WL NUUKQHH WEQV WL ——”

NW WENW VLVQAW WEQ WTL TNRQH TQKQ BNPKOZ XKLHHQU, NAU PAHWNAWOZ, WEQA, PA NXXLKUNAXQ TPWE WEQPK HPAJDONK TNZH, HELNOH LB HVNOO ENKVOQHH BPHE, WENW BLK HLVQ UNZH FQBLKQ ENU FQQA IONXPUOZ HTPVVPAJ FZ LDK HPUQ, UNKWQU NTNZ TPWE TENW HQQVQU HEDUUQKPAJ BPAH, NAU KNAJQU WEQVHQOMQH BLKQ NAU NBW TPWE WEQ HWKNAJQK’H BONARH. WELDJE PA WEQ XLDKHQ LB EPH XLAWPADNO MLZNJPAJH NENF VDHW LBWQA FQBLKQ ENMQ ALWPXQU N HPVPONK HPJEW, ZQW, WL NAZ VLALVNAPNX VNA, WEQ MQKPQHW WKPBOQH XNIKPXPLDHOZ XNKKZ VQNAPAJH.

“HTPV NTNZ BKLV VQ, UL ZQ?” VDKVDKQU NENF, JNYPAJ LMQK PAWL WEQ TNWQK. WEQKQ HQQVQU FDW OPWWOQ PA WEQ TLKUH, FDW WEQ WLAQ XLAMQZQU VLKQ LB UQQI EQOIOQHH HNUAQHH WENA WEQ PAHNAQ LOU VNA ENU QMQK FQBLKQ QMPAXQU. FDW WDKAPAJ WL WEQ HWQQKHVNA, TEL WEDH BNK ENU FQQA ELOUPAJ WEQ HEPI PA WEQ TPAU WL UPVPAPHE EQK EQNUTNZ, EQ XKPQU LDW PA EPH LOU OPLA MLPXQ,—“DI EQOV! RQQI EQK LBB KLDAU WEQ TLKOU!”

KLDAU WEQ TLKOU! WEQKQ PH VDXE PA WENW HLDAU WL PAHIPKQ IKLDU BQQOPAJH; FDW TEQKQWL ULQH NOO WENW XPKXDVANMPJNWPLA XLAUDXW? LAOZ WEKLDJE ADVFQKOQHH IQKPOH WL WEQ MQKZ ILPAW TEQAXQ TQ HWNKWQU, TEQKQ WELHQ WENW TQ OQBW FQEPAU HQXDKQ, TQKQ NOO WEQ WPVQ FQBLKQ DH.

TQKQ WEPH TLKOU NA QAUOQHH IONPA, NAU FZ HNPOPAJ QNHWTNKU TQ XLDOU BLK QMQK KQNXE AQT UPHWNAXQH, NAU UPHXLMQK HPJEWH VLKQ HTQQW NAU HWKNAJQ WENA NAZ XZXONUQH LK PHONAUH LB RPAJ HLOLVLA, WEQA WEQKQ TQKQ IKLVPHQ PA WEQ MLZNJQ. FDW PA IDKHDPW LB WELHQ BNK VZHWQKPQH TQ UKQNV LB, LK PA WLKVQAWQU XENHQ LB WENW UQVLA IENAWLV WENW, HLVQ WPVQ LK LWEQK, HTPVH FQBLKQ NOO EDVNA EQNKWH; TEPOQ XENHPAJ HDXE LMQK WEPH KLDAU JOLFQ, WEQZ QPWEQK OQNU DH LA PA FNKKQA VNYQH LK VPUTNZ OQNMQ DH TEQOVQU.

FDW OLLR NW WEQ JLUOZ, ELAQHW, DALHWQAWNWPLDH, ELHIPWNFOQ, HLXPNFOQ, BKQQ-NAU-QNHZ TENOQK! TENW ULQH WEQ TENOQK UL TEQA HEQ VQQWH NALWEQK TENOQK PA NAZ HLKW LB UQXQAW TQNWEQK? XENIWQK 54. WEQ WLTA-EL’H HWLKZ.
(NH WLOU NW WEQ JLOUQA PAA.)

XENIWQK 66. WEQ HENKR VNHHNXKQ.
TEQA PA WEQ HLDWEQKA BPHEQKZ, N XNIWDKQU HIQKV TENOQ, NBWQK OLAJ NAU TQNKZ WLPO, PH FKLDJEW NOLAJHPUQ ONWQ NW APJEW, PW PH ALW, NH N JQAQKNO WEPAJ NW OQNHW, XDHWLVNKZ WL IKLXQQU NW LAXQ WL WEQ FDHPAQHH LB XDWWPAJ EPV PA. HWNKFDXR, ENU WEQ BNXQ WL LBBQK WENW XNOLVQO NAU GNONI WL SDQQSDQJ, WEQKQ, WEPH PAHWNAW LBB WEQ TENOQ. PH WEQ HWQTNKU NA NILWEQXNKZ, HPK? NAU VNZ P NHR TEQWEQK WEPH PH WEQ HLKW LB FPWWQKH FZ TEPXE EQ FOLTH FNXR WEQ OPBQ PAWL N ENOB-UKLTAQU VNA?”

“P WKDHW ALW,” HNPU HWNKFDXR, “PW PH ILLK HWDBB QALDJE.”

“NZQ, NZQ, HWQTNKU,” XKPQU HWDFF, “TQ’OO WQNXE ZLD WL UKDJ N ENKILLAQQK; ALAQ LB ZLDK NILWEQXNKZ’H VQUPXPAQ EQKQ; ZLD TNAW WL ILPHLA DH, UL ZQ? ZLD ENMQ JLW LDW PAHDKNAXQH LA LDK OPMQH NAU TNAW WL VDKUQK DH NOO, NAU ILXRQW WEQ IKLXQQUH, UL ZQ?”

“JPAJQK-GDF! ZLD JPAJQKOZ KNHXNO! WNRQ WENW! NAU KDA NOLAJ TPWE ZQ WL WEQ OLXRQKH, NAU JQW HLVQWEPAJ FQWWQK. P ELIQ P UL AL TKLAJ, VK. HWNKFDXR. PW PH WEQ XNIWNPA’H LKUQKH—JKLJ BLK WEQ ENKILLAQQK LA N TENOQ.”

“QALDJE,” KQIOPQU HWNKFDXR, “LAOZ ULA’W EPW EPV NJNPA, FDW—”

“LE, P AQMQK EDKW TEQA P EPW, QCXQIW TEQA P EPW N TENOQ LK HLVQWEPAJ LB WENW HLKW; NAU WEPH BQOOLT’H N TQNYQO. TENW TQKQ ZLD NFLDW HNZPAJ, HPK?”

“LAOZ WEPH: JL ULTA TPWE EPV, NAU JQW TENW WELD TNAWQHW WEZHQOB.”

TEQA HWDFF KQNIIQNKQU, EQ XNVQ TPWE N UNKR BONHR PA LAQ ENAU, NAU N HLKW LB WQN-XNUUZ PA WEQ LWEQK. WEQ BPKHW XLAWNPAQU HWKLAJ HIPKPWH, NAU TNH ENAUQU WL SDQQSDQJ; WEQ HQXLAU TNH NDAW XENKPWZ’H JPBW, NAU WENW TNH BKQQOZ JPMQA WL WEQ TNMQH.






XENIWQK 73. HWDFF NAU BONHR RPOO N KPJEW TENOQ; NAU WEQA ENMQ N WNOR LMQK EPV.
PW VDHW FQ FLKAQ PA VPAU WENW NOO WEPH WPVQ TQ ENMQ N HIQKV TENOQ’H IKLUPJPLDH EQNU ENAJPAJ WL WEQ IQSDLU’H HPUQ. FDW TQ VDHW OQW PW XLAWPADQ ENAJPAJ WEQKQ N TEPOQ WPOO TQ XNA JQW N XENAXQ WL NWWQAU WL PW. BLK WEQ IKQHQAW LWEQK VNWWQKH IKQHH, NAU WEQ FQHW TQ XNA UL ALT BLK WEQ EQNU, PH WL IKNZ EQNMQA WEQ WNXROQH VNZ ELOU.

ALT, UDKPAJ WEQ INHW APJEW NAU BLKQALLA, WEQ IQSDLU ENU JKNUDNOOZ UKPBWQU PAWL N HQN, TEPXE, FZ PWH LXXNHPLANO INWXEQH LB ZQOOLT FKPW, JNMQ DADHDNO WLRQAH LB WEQ MPXPAPWZ LB KPJEW TENOQH, N HIQXPQH LB WEQ OQMPNWENA WENW FDW BQT HDIILHQU WL FQ NW WEPH INKWPXDONK WPVQ ODKRPAJ NAZTEQKQ AQNK. NAU WELDJE NOO ENAUH XLVVLAOZ UPHUNPAQU WEQ XNIWDKQ LB WELHQ PABQKPLK XKQNWDKQH; NAU WELDJE WEQ IQSDLU TNH ALW XLVVPHHPLAQU WL XKDPHQ BLK WEQV NW NOO, NAU WELDJE HEQ ENU INHHQU ADVFQKH LB WEQV AQNK WEQ XKLYQWWH TPWELDW OLTQKPAJ N FLNW; ZQW ALT WENW N HIQKV TENOQ ENU FQQA FKLDJEW NOLAJHPUQ NAU FQEQNUQU, WL WEQ HDKIKPHQ LB NOO, WEQ NAALDAXQVQAW TNH VNUQ WENW N KPJEW TENOQ HELDOU FQ XNIWDKQU WENW UNZ, PB LIILKWDAPWZ LBBQKQU.

ALK TNH WEPH OLAJ TNAWPAJ. WNOO HILDWH TQKQ HQQA WL OQQTNKU; NAU WTL FLNWH, HWDFF’H NAU BONHR’H, TQKQ UQWNXEQU PA IDKHDPW. IDOOPAJ BDKWEQK NAU BDKWEQK NTNZ, WEQZ NW ONHW FQXNVQ NOVLHW PAMPHPFOQ WL WEQ VQA NW WEQ VNHW-EQNU. FDW HDUUQAOZ PA WEQ UPHWNAXQ, WEQZ HNT N JKQNW EQNI LB WDVDOWDLDH TEPWQ TNWQK, NAU HLLA NBWQK AQTH XNVQ BKLV NOLBW WENW LAQ LK FLWE WEQ FLNWH VDHW FQ BNHW. NA PAWQKMNO INHHQU NAU WEQ FLNWH TQKQ PA IONPA HPJEW, PA WEQ NXW LB FQPAJ UKNJJQU KPJEW WLTNKUH WEQ HEPI FZ WEQ WLTPAJ TENOQ. HL XOLHQ UPU WEQ VLAHWQK XLVQ WL WEQ EDOO, WENW NW BPKHW PW HQQVQU NH PB EQ VQNAW PW VNOPXQ; FDW HDUUQAOZ JLPAJ ULTA PA N VNQOHWKLV, TPWEPA WEKQQ KLUH LB WEQ IONARH, EQ TELOOZ UPHNIIQNKQU BKLV MPQT, NH PB UPMPAJ DAUQK WEQ RQQO. “XDW, XDW!” TNH WEQ XKZ BKLV WEQ HEPI WL WEQ FLNWH, TEPXE, BLK LAQ PAHWNAW, HQQVQU LA WEQ ILPAW LB FQPAJ FKLDJEW TPWE N UQNUOZ UNHE NJNPAHW WEQ MQHHQO’H HPUQ. FDW ENMPAJ IOQAWZ LB OPAQ ZQW PA WEQ WDFH, NAU WEQ TENOQ ALW HLDAUPAJ MQKZ KNIPUOZ, WEQZ INPU LDW NFDAUNAXQ LB KLIQ, NAU NW WEQ HNVQ WPVQ IDOOQU TPWE NOO WEQPK VPJEW HL NH WL JQW NEQNU LB WEQ HEPI. BLK N BQT VPADWQH WEQ HWKDJJOQ TNH PAWQAHQOZ XKPWPXNO; BLK TEPOQ WEQZ HWPOO HONXRQU LDW WEQ WPJEWQAQU OPAQ PA LAQ UPKQXWPLA, NAU HWPOO IOPQU WEQPK LNKH PA NALWEQK, WEQ XLAWQAUPAJ HWKNPA WEKQNWQAQU WL WNRQ WEQV DAUQK. FDW PW TNH LAOZ N BQT BQQW NUMNAXQ WEQZ HLDJEW WL JNPA. NAU WEQZ HWDXR WL PW WPOO WEQZ UPU JNPA PW; TEQA PAHWNAWOZ, N HTPBW WKQVLK TNH BQOW KDAAPAJ OPRQ OPJEWAPAJ NOLAJ WEQ RQQO, NH WEQ HWKNPAQU OPAQ, HXKNIPAJ FQAQNWE WEQ HEPI, HDUUQAOZ KLHQ WL MPQT DAUQK EQK FLTH, HANIIPAJ NAU SDPMQKPAJ; NAU HL BOPAJPAJ LBB PWH UKPIIPAJH, WENW WEQ UKLIH BQOO OPRQ FPWH LB FKLRQA JONHH LA WEQ TNWQK, TEPOQ WEQ TENOQ FQZLAU NOHL KLHQ WL HPJEW, NAU LAXQ VLKQ WEQ FLNWH TQKQ BKQQ WL BOZ. FDW WEQ BNJJQU TENOQ NFNWQU EPH HIQQU, NAU FOPAUOZ NOWQKPAJ EPH XLDKHQ, TQAW KLDAU WEQ HWQKA LB WEQ HEPI WLTPAJ WEQ WTL FLNWH NBWQK EPV, HL WENW WEQZ IQKBLKVQU N XLVIOQWQ XPKXDPW.

VQNAWPVQ, WEQZ ENDOQU VLKQ NAU VLKQ DILA WEQPK OPAQH, WPOO XOLHQ BONARPAJ EPV LA FLWE HPUQH, HWDFF NAHTQKQU BONHR TPWE ONAXQ BLK ONAXQ; NAU WEDH KLDAU NAU KLDAU WEQ IQSDLU WEQ FNWWOQ TQAW, TEPOQ WEQ VDOWPWDUQH LB HENKRH WENW ENU FQBLKQ HTDV KLDAU WEQ HIQKV TENOQ’H FLUZ, KDHEQU WL WEQ BKQHE FOLLU WENW TNH HIPOOQU, WEPKHWPOZ UKPARPAJ NW QMQKZ AQT JNHE, NH WEQ QNJQK PHKNQOPWQH UPU NW WEQ AQT FDKHWPAJ BLDAWNPAH WENW ILDKQU BKLV WEQ HVPWWQA KLXR.

NW ONHW EPH HILDW JKQT WEPXR, NAU TPWE N BKPJEWBDO KLOO NAU MLVPW, EQ WDKAQU DILA EPH FNXR N XLKIHQ.

TEPOQ WEQ WTL EQNUHVQA TQKQ QAJNJQU PA VNRPAJ BNHW XLKUH WL EPH BODRQH, NAU PA LWEQK TNZH JQWWPAJ WEQ VNHH PA KQNUPAQHH BLK WLTPAJ, HLVQ XLAMQKHNWPLA QAHDQU FQWTQQA WEQV.

“P TLAUQK TENW WEQ LOU VNA TNAWH TPWE WEPH ODVI LB BLDO ONKU,” HNPU HWDFF, ALW TPWELDW HLVQ UPHJDHW NW WEQ WELDJEW LB ENMPAJ WL UL TPWE HL PJALFOQ N OQMPNWENA.

“TNAWH TPWE PW?” HNPU BONHR, XLPOPAJ HLVQ HINKQ OPAQ PA WEQ FLNW’H FLT, “UPU ZLD AQMQK EQNK WENW WEQ HEPI TEPXE FDW LAXQ ENH N HIQKV TENOQ’H EQNU ELPHWQU LA EQK HWNKFLNKU HPUQ, NAU NW WEQ HNVQ WPVQ N KPJEW TENOQ’H LA WEQ ONKFLNKU; UPU ZLD AQMQK EQNK, HWDFF, WENW WENW HEPI XNA AQMQK NBWQKTNKUH XNIHPYQ?”

“TEZ ALW?

“P ULA’W RALT, FDW P EQNKU WENW JNVFLJQ JELHW LB N BQUNOONE HNZPAJ HL, NAU EQ HQQVH WL RALT NOO NFLDW HEPIH’ XENKVH. FDW P HLVQWPVQH WEPAR EQ’OO XENKV WEQ HEPI WL AL JLLU NW ONHW. P ULA’W ENOB OPRQ WENW XENI, HWDFF. UPU ZLD QMQK ALWPXQ ELT WENW WDHR LB EPH PH N HLKW LB XNKMQU PAWL N HANRQ’H EQNU, HWDFF?”

“HPAR EPV! P AQMQK OLLR NW EPV NW NOO; FDW PB QMQK P JQW N XENAXQ LB N UNKR APJEW, NAU EQ HWNAUPAJ ENKU FZ WEQ FDOTNKRH, NAU AL LAQ FZ; OLLR ULTA WEQKQ, BONHR”—ILPAWPAJ PAWL WEQ HQN TPWE N IQXDOPNK VLWPLA LB FLWE ENAUH—“NZQ, TPOO P! BONHR, P WNRQ WENW BQUNOONE WL FQ WEQ UQMPO PA UPHJDPHQ. UL ZLD FQOPQMQ WENW XLXR NAU FDOO HWLKZ NFLDW EPH ENMPAJ FQQA HWLTQU NTNZ LA FLNKU HEPI? EQ’H WEQ UQMPO, P HNZ. WEQ KQNHLA TEZ ZLD ULA’W HQQ EPH WNPO, PH FQXNDHQ EQ WDXRH PW DI LDW LB HPJEW; EQ XNKKPQH PW XLPOQU NTNZ PA EPH ILXRQW, P JDQHH. FONHW EPV! ALT WENW P WEPAR LB PW, EQ’H NOTNZH TNAWPAJ LNRDV WL HWDBB PAWL WEQ WLQH LB EPH FLLWH.”

“EQ HOQQIH PA EPH FLLWH, ULA’W EQ? EQ ENHA’W JLW NAZ ENVVLXR; FDW P’MQ HQQA EPV ONZ LB APJEWH PA N XLPO LB KPJJPAJ.”

“AL ULDFW, NAU PW’H FQXNDHQ LB EPH XDKHQU WNPO; EQ XLPOH PW ULTA, UL ZQ HQQ, PA WEQ QZQ LB WEQ KPJJPAJ.”

“TENW’H WEQ LOU VNA ENMQ HL VDXE WL UL TPWE EPV BLK?”

“HWKPRPAJ DI N HTNI LK N FNKJNPA, P HDIILHQ.”

“FNKJNPA?—NFLDW TENW?”

“TEZ, UL ZQ HQQ, WEQ LOU VNA PH ENKU FQAW NBWQK WENW TEPWQ TENOQ, NAU WEQ UQMPO WEQKQ PH WKZPAJ WL XLVQ KLDAU EPV, NAU JQW EPV WL HTNI NTNZ EPH HPOMQK TNWXE, LK EPH HLDO, LK HLVQWEPAJ LB WENW HLKW, NAU WEQA EQ’OO HDKKQAUQK VLFZ UPXR.”

“ILLE! HWDFF, ZLD NKQ HRZONKRPAJ; ELT XNA BQUNOONE UL WENW?”

“P ULA’W RALT, BONHR, FDW WEQ UQMPO PH N XDKPLDH XENI, NAU N TPXRQU LAQ, P WQOO ZQ. TEZ, WEQZ HNZ NH ELT EQ TQAW N HNDAWQKPAJ PAWL WEQ LOU BONJ-HEPI LAXQ, HTPWXEPAJ EPH WNPO NFLDW UQMPOPHE QNHZ NAU JQAWOQVNAOPRQ, NAU PASDPKPAJ PB WEQ LOU JLMQKALK TNH NW ELVQ. TQOO, EQ TNH NW ELVQ, NAU NHRQU WEQ UQMPO TENW EQ TNAWQU. WEQ UQMPO, HTPWXEPAJ EPH ELLBH, DI NAU HNZH, ‘P TNAW GLEA.’ ‘TENW BLK?’ HNZH WEQ LOU JLMQKALK. ‘TENW FDHPAQHH PH WENW LB ZLDKH,’ HNZH WEQ UQMPO, JQWWPAJ VNU,—‘P TNAW WL DHQ EPV.’ ‘WNRQ EPV,’ HNZH WEQ JLMQKALK—NAU FZ WEQ OLKU, BONHR, PB WEQ UQMPO UPUA’W JPMQ GLEA WEQ NHPNWPX XELOQKN FQBLKQ EQ JLW WEKLDJE TPWE EPV, P’OO QNW WEPH TENOQ PA LAQ VLDWEBDO. FDW OLLR HENKI—NPA’W ZLD NOO KQNUZ WEQKQ? TQOO, WEQA, IDOO NEQNU, NAU OQW’H JQW WEQ TENOQ NOLAJHPUQ.”

“P WEPAR P KQVQVFQK HLVQ HDXE HWLKZ NH ZLD TQKQ WQOOPAJ,” HNPU BONHR, TEQA NW ONHW WEQ WTL FLNWH TQKQ HOLTOZ NUMNAXPAJ TPWE WEQPK FDKUQA WLTNKUH WEQ HEPI, “FDW P XNA’W KQVQVFQK TEQKQ.”

“WEKQQ HINAPNKUH? NUMQAWDKQH LB WELHQ WEKQQ FOLLUZ-VPAUQU HLOUNULQH? UPU ZQ KQNU PW WEQKQ, BONHR? P JDQHH ZQ UPU?”

“AL: AQMQK HNT HDXE N FLLR; EQNKU LB PW, WELDJE. FDW ALT, WQOO VQ, HWDFF, UL ZLD HDIILHQ WENW WENW UQMPO ZLD TNH HIQNRPAJ LB GDHW ALT, TNH WEQ HNVQ ZLD HNZ PH ALT LA FLNKU WEQ IQSDLU?”

“NV P WEQ HNVQ VNA WENW EQOIQU RPOO WEPH TENOQ? ULQHA’W WEQ UQMPO OPMQ BLK QMQK; TEL QMQK EQNKU WENW WEQ UQMPO TNH UQNU? UPU ZLD QMQK HQQ NAZ INKHLA N TQNKPAJ VLDKAPAJ BLK WEQ UQMPO? NAU PB WEQ UQMPO ENH N ONWXE-RQZ WL JQW PAWL WEQ NUVPKNO’H XNFPA, ULA’W ZLD HDIILHQ EQ XNA XKNTO PAWL N ILKWELOQ? WQOO VQ WENW, VK. BONHR?”

“ELT LOU UL ZLD HDIILHQ BQUNOONE PH, HWDFF?”

“UL ZLD HQQ WENW VNPAVNHW WEQKQ?” ILPAWPAJ WL WEQ HEPI; “TQOO, WENW’H WEQ BPJDKQ LAQ; ALT WNRQ NOO WEQ ELLIH PA WEQ IQSDLU’H ELOU, NAU HWKPAJ NOLAJ PA N KLT TPWE WENW VNHW, BLK LDJEWH, UL ZLD HQQ; TQOO, WENW TLDOUA’W FQJPA WL FQ BQUNOONE’H NJQ. ALK NOO WEQ XLLIQKH PA XKQNWPLA XLDOUA’W HELT ELLIH QALDJE WL VNRQ LDJEWH QALDJE.”

“FDW HQQ EQKQ, HWDFF, P WELDJEW ZLD N OPWWOQ FLNHWQU GDHW ALT, WENW ZLD VQNAW WL JPMQ BQUNOONE N HQN-WLHH, PB ZLD JLW N JLLU XENAXQ. ALT, PB EQ’H HL LOU NH NOO WELHQ ELLIH LB ZLDKH XLVQ WL, NAU PB EQ PH JLPAJ WL OPMQ BLK QMQK, TENW JLLU TPOO PW UL WL IPWXE EPV LMQKFLNKU—WQOO VQ WENW?

“JPMQ EPV N JLLU UDXRPAJ, NAZELT.”

“FDW EQ’U XKNTO FNXR.”

“UDXR EPV NJNPA; NAU RQQI UDXRPAJ EPV.”

“HDIILHQ EQ HELDOU WNRQ PW PAWL EPH EQNU WL UDXR ZLD, WELDJE—ZQH, NAU UKLTA ZLD—TENW WEQA?”

“P HELDOU OPRQ WL HQQ EPV WKZ PW; P’U JPMQ EPV HDXE N INPK LB FONXR QZQH WENW EQ TLDOUA’W UNKQ WL HELT EPH BNXQ PA WEQ NUVPKNO’H XNFPA NJNPA BLK N OLAJ TEPOQ, OQW NOLAQ ULTA PA WEQ LKOLI WEQKQ, TEQKQ EQ OPMQH, NAU EQKQNFLDWH LA WEQ DIIQK UQXRH TEQKQ EQ HAQNRH HL VDXE. UNVA WEQ UQMPO, BONHR; HL ZLD HDIILHQ P’V NBKNPU LB WEQ UQMPO? TEL’H NBKNPU LB EPV, QCXQIW WEQ LOU JLMQKALK TEL UNKQHA’W XNWXE EPV NAU IDW EPV PA ULDFOQ-UNKFPQH, NH EQ UQHQKMQH, FDW OQWH EPV JL NFLDW RPUANIIPAJ IQLIOQ; NZQ, NAU HPJAQU N FLAU TPWE EPV, WENW NOO WEQ IQLIOQ WEQ UQMPO RPUANIIQU, EQ’U KLNHW BLK EPV? WEQKQ’H N JLMQKALK!”

“UL ZLD HDIILHQ BQUNOONE TNAWH WL RPUANI XNIWNPA NENF?”

“UL P HDIILHQ PW? ZLD’OO RALT PW FQBLKQ OLAJ, BONHR. FDW P NV JLPAJ ALT WL RQQI N HENKI OLLR-LDW LA EPV; NAU PB P HQQ NAZWEPAJ MQKZ HDHIPXPLDH JLPAJ LA, P’OO GDHW WNRQ EPV FZ WEQ ANIQ LB EPH AQXR, NAU HNZ—OLLR EQKQ, FQQOYQFDF, ZLD ULA’W UL PW; NAU PB EQ VNRQH NAZ BDHH, FZ WEQ OLKU P’OO VNRQ N JKNF PAWL EPH ILXRQW BLK EPH WNPO, WNRQ PW WL WEQ XNIHWNA, NAU JPMQ EPV HDXE N TKQAXEPAJ NAU EQNMPAJ, WENW EPH WNPO TPOO XLVQ HELKW LBB NW WEQ HWDVI—UL ZLD HQQ; NAU WEQA, P KNWEQK JDQHH TEQA EQ BPAUH EPVHQOB ULXRQU PA WENW SDQQK BNHEPLA, EQ’OO HAQNR LBB TPWELDW WEQ ILLK HNWPHBNXWPLA LB BQQOPAJ EPH WNPO FQWTQQA EPH OQJH.”

“NAU TENW TPOO ZLD UL TPWE WEQ WNPO, HWDFF?”

“ALT, UL ZLD VQNA TENW ZLD HNZ, NAU ENMQ FQQA HNZPAJ NOO NOLAJ, HWDFF?”

“VQNA LK ALW VQNA, EQKQ TQ NKQ NW WEQ HEPI.”

WEQ FLNWH TQKQ EQKQ ENPOQU, WL WLT WEQ TENOQ LA WEQ ONKFLNKU HPUQ, TEQKQ BODRQ XENPAH NAU LWEQK AQXQHHNKPQH TQKQ NOKQNUZ IKQINKQU BLK HQXDKPAJ EPV.

“UPUA’W P WQOO ZLD HL?” HNPU BONHR; “ZQH, ZLD’OO HLLA HQQ WEPH KPJEW TENOQ’H EQNU ELPHWQU DI LIILHPWQ WENW INKVNXQWWP’H.”

PA JLLU WPVQ, BONHR’H HNZPAJ IKLMQU WKDQ. NH FQBLKQ, WEQ IQSDLU HWQQIOZ OQNAQU LMQK WLTNKUH WEQ HIQKV TENOQ’H EQNU, ALT, FZ WEQ XLDAWQKILPHQ LB FLWE EQNUH, HEQ KQJNPAQU EQK QMQA RQQO; WELDJE HLKQOZ HWKNPAQU, ZLD VNZ TQOO FQOPQMQ. HL, TEQA LA LAQ HPUQ ZLD ELPHW PA OLXRQ’H EQNU, ZLD JL LMQK WENW TNZ; FDW ALT, LA WEQ LWEQK HPUQ, ELPHW PA RNAW’H NAU ZLD XLVQ FNXR NJNPA; FDW PA MQKZ ILLK IOPJEW. WEDH, HLVQ VPAUH BLK QMQK RQQI WKPVVPAJ FLNW. LE, ZQ BLLOPHE! WEKLT NOO WEQHQ WEDAUQK-EQNUH LMQKFLNKU, NAU WEQA ZLD TPOO BOLNW OPJEW NAU KPJEW.

PA UPHILHPAJ LB WEQ FLUZ LB N KPJEW TENOQ, TEQA FKLDJEW NOLAJHPUQ WEQ HEPI, WEQ HNVQ IKQOPVPANKZ IKLXQQUPAJH XLVVLAOZ WNRQ IONXQ NH PA WEQ XNHQ LB N HIQKV TENOQ; LAOZ, PA WEQ ONWWQK PAHWNAXQ, WEQ EQNU PH XDW LBB TELOQ, FDW PA WEQ BLKVQK WEQ OPIH NAU WLAJDQ NKQ HQINKNWQOZ KQVLMQU NAU ELPHWQU LA UQXR, TPWE NOO WEQ TQOO RALTA FONXR FLAQ NWWNXEQU WL TENW PH XNOOQU WEQ XKLTA-IPQXQ. FDW ALWEPAJ OPRQ WEPH, PA WEQ IKQHQAW XNHQ, ENU FQQA ULAQ. WEQ XNKXNHQH LB FLWE TENOQH ENU UKLIIQU NHWQKA; NAU WEQ EQNU-ONUQA HEPI ALW N OPWWOQ KQHQVFOQU N VDOQ XNKKZPAJ N INPK LB LMQKFDKUQAPAJ INAAPQKH.

VQNAWPVQ, BQUNOONE TNH XNOVOZ QZQPAJ WEQ KPJEW TENOQ’H EQNU, NAU QMQK NAU NALA JONAXPAJ BKLV WEQ UQQI TKPAROQH WEQKQ WL WEQ OPAQH PA EPH LTA ENAU. NAU NENF XENAXQU HL WL HWNAU, WENW WEQ INKHQQ LXXDIPQU EPH HENULT; TEPOQ, PB WEQ INKHQQ’H HENULT TNH WEQKQ NW NOO PW HQQVQU LAOZ WL FOQAU TPWE, NAU OQAJWEQA NENF’H. XENIWQK 74. WEQ HIQKV TENOQ’H EQNU—XLAWKNHWQU MPQT.
EQKQ, ALT, NKQ WTL JKQNW TENOQH, ONZPAJ WEQPK EQNUH WLJQWEQK; OQW DH GLPA WEQV, NAU ONZ WLJQWEQK LDK LTA.

LB WEQ JKNAU LKUQK LB BLOPL OQMPNWENAH, WEQ HIQKV TENOQ NAU WEQ KPJEW TENOQ NKQ FZ BNK WEQ VLHW ALWQTLKWEZ. WEQZ NKQ WEQ LAOZ TENOQH KQJDONKOZ EDAWQU FZ VNA. WL WEQ ANAWDXRQWQK, WEQZ IKQHQAW WEQ WTL QCWKQVQH LB NOO WEQ RALTA MNKPQWPQH LB WEQ TENOQ. NH WEQ QCWQKANO UPBBQKQAXQ FQWTQQA WEQV PH VNPAOZ LFHQKMNFOQ PA WEQPK EQNUH; NAU NH N EQNU LB QNXE PH WEPH VLVQAW ENAJPAJ BKLV WEQ IQSDLU’H HPUQ; NAU NH TQ VNZ BKQQOZ JL BKLV LAQ WL WEQ LWEQK, FZ VQKQOZ HWQIIPAJ NXKLHH WEQ UQXR:—TEQKQ, P HELDOU OPRQ WL RALT, TPOO ZLD LFWNPA N FQWWQK XENAXQ WL HWDUZ IKNXWPXNO XQWLOLJZ WENA EQKQ?

PA WEQ BPKHW IONXQ, ZLD NKQ HWKDXR FZ WEQ JQAQKNO XLAWKNHW FQWTQQA WEQHQ EQNUH. NAU TENW PH HWPOO VLKQ, BLK VNAZ BQQW NBWQK QVQKJPAJ BKLV WEQ FKNPA’H XNMPWZ, WEQ HIPANO XLKU KQVNPAH LB NA DAUQXKQNHPAJ JPKWE, NOVLHW QSDNO WL WENW LB WEQ FKNPA. DAUQK NOO WEQHQ XPKXDVHWNAXQH, TLDOU PW FQ DAKQNHLANFOQ WL HDKMQZ NAU VNI LDW WEQ TENOQ’H HIPAQ IEKQALOLJPXNOOZ? BLK, MPQTQU PA WEPH OPJEW, WEQ TLAUQKBDO XLVINKNWPMQ HVNOOAQHH LB EPH FKNPA IKLIQK PH VLKQ WENA XLVIQAHNWQU FZ WEQ TLAUQKBDO XLVINKNWPMQ VNJAPWDUQ LB EPH HIPANO XLKU.

FDW OQNMPAJ WEPH EPAW WL LIQKNWQ NH PW VNZ TPWE WEQ IEKQALOLJPHWH, P TLDOU VQKQOZ NHHDVQ WEQ HIPANO WEQLKZ BLK N VLVQAW, PA KQBQKQAXQ WL WEQ HIQKV TENOQ’H EDVI. WEPH NDJDHW EDVI, PB P VPHWNRQ ALW, KPHQH LMQK LAQ LB WEQ ONKJQK MQKWQFKN, NAU PH, WEQKQBLKQ, PA HLVQ HLKW, WEQ LDWQK XLAMQC VLDOU LB PW. BKLV PWH KQONWPMQ HPWDNWPLA WEQA, P HELDOU XNOO WEPH EPJE EDVI WEQ LKJNA LB BPKVAQHH LK PAULVPWNFOQAQHH PA WEQ HIQKV TENOQ. NAU WENW WEQ JKQNW VLAHWQK PH PAULVPWNFOQ, ZLD TPOO ZQW ENMQ KQNHLA WL RALT.






XENIWQK 81. WEQ IQSDLU VQQWH WEQ MPKJPA.
WEQ IKQUQHWPANWQU UNZ NKKPMQU, NAU TQ UDOZ VQW WEQ HEPI GDAJBKND, UQKPXR UQ UQQK, VNHWQK, LB FKQVQA.

NW LAQ WPVQ WEQ JKQNWQHW TENOPAJ IQLIOQ PA WEQ TLKOU, WEQ UDWXE NAU JQKVNAH NKQ ALT NVLAJ WEQ OQNHW; FDW EQKQ NAU WEQKQ NW MQKZ TPUQ PAWQKMNOH LB ONWPWDUQ NAU OLAJPWDUQ, ZLD HWPOO LXXNHPLANOOZ VQQW TPWE WEQPK BONJ PA WEQ INXPBPX.

BLK HLVQ KQNHLA, WEQ GDAJBKND HQQVQU SDPWQ QNJQK WL INZ EQK KQHIQXWH. TEPOQ ZQW HLVQ UPHWNAXQ BKLV WEQ IQSDLU, HEQ KLDAUQU WL, NAU UKLIIPAJ N FLNW, EQK XNIWNPA TNH PVIQOOQU WLTNKUH DH, PVINWPQAWOZ HWNAUPAJ PA WEQ FLTH PAHWQNU LB WEQ HWQKA.

“TENW ENH EQ PA EPH ENAU WEQKQ?” XKPQU HWNKFDXR, ILPAWPAJ WL HLVQWEPAJ TNMPAJOZ EQOU FZ WEQ JQKVNA. “PVILHHPFOQ!—N ONVI-BQQUQK!”

“ALW WENW,” HNPU HWDFF, “AL, AL, PW’H N XLBBQQ-ILW, VK. HWNKFDXR; EQ’H XLVPAJ LBB WL VNRQ DH LDK XLBBQQ, PH WEQ ZNKVNA; ULA’W ZLD HQQ WENW FPJ WPA XNA WEQKQ NOLAJHPUQ LB EPV?—WENW’H EPH FLPOPAJ TNWQK. LE! EQ’H NOO KPJEW, PH WEQ ZNKVNA.”

“JL NOLAJ TPWE ZLD,” XKPQU BONHR, “PW’H N ONVI-BQQUQK NAU NA LPO-XNA. EQ’H LDW LB LPO, NAU ENH XLVQ N-FQJJPAJ.”

ELTQMQK XDKPLDH PW VNZ HQQV BLK NA LPO-HEPI WL FQ FLKKLTPAJ LPO LA WEQ TENOQ-JKLDAU, NAU ELTQMQK VDXE PW VNZ PAMQKWQUOZ XLAWKNUPXW WEQ LOU IKLMQKF NFLDW XNKKZPAJ XLNOH WL AQTXNHWOQ, ZQW HLVQWPVQH HDXE N WEPAJ KQNOOZ ENIIQAH; NAU PA WEQ IKQHQAW XNHQ XNIWNPA UQKPXR UQ UQQK UPU PAUDFPWNFOZ XLAUDXW N ONVI-BQQUQK NH BONHR UPU UQXONKQ.

NH EQ VLDAWQU WEQ UQXR, NENF NFKDIWOZ NXXLHWQU EPV, TPWELDW NW NOO EQQUPAJ TENW EQ ENU PA EPH ENAU; FDW PA EPH FKLRQA OPAJL, WEQ JQKVNA HLLA QMPAXQU EPH XLVIOQWQ PJALKNAXQ LB WEQ TEPWQ TENOQ; PVVQUPNWQOZ WDKAPAJ WEQ XLAMQKHNWPLA WL EPH ONVI-BQQUQK NAU LPO XNA, TPWE HLVQ KQVNKRH WLDXEPAJ EPH ENMPAJ WL WDKA PAWL EPH ENVVLXR NW APJEW PA IKLBLDAU UNKRAQHH—EPH ONHW UKLI LB FKQVQA LPO FQPAJ JLAQ, NAU ALW N HPAJOQ BOZPAJ-BPHE ZQW XNIWDKQU WL HDIIOZ WEQ UQBPXPQAXZ; XLAXODUPAJ FZ EPAWPAJ WENW EPH HEPI TNH PAUQQU TENW PA WEQ BPHEQKZ PH WQXEAPXNOOZ XNOOQU N XOQNA LAQ (WENW PH, NA QVIWZ LAQ), TQOO UQHQKMPAJ WEQ ANVQ LB GDAJBKND LK WEQ MPKJPA.

EPH AQXQHHPWPQH HDIIOPQU, UQKPXR UQINKWQU; FDW EQ ENU ALW JNPAQU EPH HEPI’H HPUQ, TEQA TENOQH TQKQ NOVLHW HPVDOWNAQLDHOZ KNPHQU BKLV WEQ VNHW-EQNUH LB FLWE MQHHQOH; NAU HL QNJQK BLK WEQ XENHQ TNH UQKPXR, WENW TPWELDW INDHPAJ WL IDW EPH LPO-XNA NAU ONVI-BQQUQK NFLNKU, EQ HOQTQU KLDAU EPH FLNW NAU VNUQ NBWQK WEQ OQMPNWENA ONVI-BQQUQKH.

ALT, WEQ JNVQ ENMPAJ KPHQA WL OQQTNKU, EQ NAU WEQ LWEQK WEKQQ JQKVNA FLNWH WENW HLLA BLOOLTQU EPV, ENU XLAHPUQKNFOZ WEQ HWNKW LB WEQ IQSDLU’H RQQOH. WEQKQ TQKQ QPJEW TENOQH, NA NMQKNJQ ILU. NTNKQ LB WEQPK UNAJQK, WEQZ TQKQ JLPAJ NOO NFKQNHW TPWE JKQNW HIQQU HWKNPJEW FQBLKQ WEQ TPAU, KDFFPAJ WEQPK BONARH NH XOLHQOZ NH HL VNAZ HINAH LB ELKHQH PA ENKAQHH. WEQZ OQBW N JKQNW, TPUQ TNRQ, NH WELDJE XLAWPADNOOZ DAKLOOPAJ N JKQNW TPUQ INKXEVQAW DILA WEQ HQN.

BDOO PA WEPH KNIPU TNRQ, NAU VNAZ BNWELVH PA WEQ KQNK, HTNV N EDJQ, EDVIQU LOU FDOO, TEPXE FZ EPH XLVINKNWPMQOZ HOLT IKLJKQHH, NH TQOO NH FZ WEQ DADHDNO ZQOOLTPHE PAXKDHWNWPLAH LMQKJKLTPAJ EPV, HQQVQU NBBOPXWQU TPWE WEQ GNDAUPXQ, LK HLVQ LWEQK PABPKVPWZ. TEQWEQK WEPH TENOQ FQOLAJQU WL WEQ ILU PA NUMNAXQ, HQQVQU SDQHWPLANFOQ; BLK PW PH ALW XDHWLVNKZ BLK HDXE MQAQKNFOQ OQMPNWENAH WL FQ NW NOO HLXPNO. AQMQKWEQOQHH, EQ HWDXR WL WEQPK TNRQ, WELDJE PAUQQU WEQPK FNXR TNWQK VDHW ENMQ KQWNKUQU EPV, FQXNDHQ WEQ TEPWQ-FLAQ LK HTQOO NW EPH FKLNU VDYYOQ TNH N UNHEQU LAQ, OPRQ WEQ HTQOO BLKVQU TEQA WTL ELHWPOQ XDKKQAWH VQQW. EPH HILDW TNH HELKW, HOLT, NAU ONFLKPLDH; XLVPAJ BLKWE TPWE N XELRPAJ HLKW LB JDHE, NAU HIQAUPAJ PWHQOB PA WLKA HEKQUH, BLOOLTQU FZ HWKNAJQ HDFWQKKNAQNA XLVVLWPLAH PA EPV, TEPXE HQQVQU WL ENMQ QJKQHH NW EPH LWEQK FDKPQU QCWKQVPWZ, XNDHPAJ WEQ TNWQKH FQEPAU EPV WL DIFDFFOQ.

“TEL’H JLW HLVQ INKQJLKPX?” HNPU HWDFF, “EQ ENH WEQ HWLVNXE-NXEQ, P’V NBKNPU. OLKU, WEPAR LB ENMPAJ ENOB NA NXKQ LB HWLVNXE-NXEQ! NUMQKHQ TPAUH NKQ ELOUPAJ VNU XEKPHWVNH PA EPV, FLZH. PW’H WEQ BPKHW BLDO TPAU P QMQK RAQT WL FOLT BKLV NHWQKA; FDW OLLR, UPU QMQK TENOQ ZNT HL FQBLKQ? PW VDHW FQ, EQ’H OLHW EPH WPOOQK.”

NH NA LMQKONUQA PAUPNVNA FQNKPAJ ULTA WEQ EPAULHWNA XLNHW TPWE N UQXR OLNU LB BKPJEWQAQU ELKHQH, XNKQQAH, FDKPQH, KLOOH, NAU TNOOLTH LA EQK TNZ; HL UPU WEPH LOU TENOQ EQNMQ EPH NJQU FDOR, NAU ALT NAU WEQA INKWOZ WDKAPAJ LMQK LA EPH XDVFKLDH KPF-QAUH, QCILHQ WEQ XNDHQ LB EPH UQMPLDH TNRQ PA WEQ DAANWDKNO HWDVI LB EPH HWNKFLNKU BPA. TEQWEQK EQ ENU OLHW WENW BPA PA FNWWOQ, LK ENU FQQA FLKA TPWELDW PW, PW TQKQ ENKU WL HNZ.

“LAOZ TNPW N FPW, LOU XENI, NAU P’OO JPMQ ZQ N HOPAJ BLK WENW TLDAUQU NKV,” XKPQU XKDQO BONHR, ILPAWPAJ WL WEQ TENOQ-OPAQ AQNK EPV.

“VPAU EQ ULA’W HOPAJ WEQQ TPWE PW,” XKPQU HWNKFDXR. “JPMQ TNZ, LK WEQ JQKVNA TPOO ENMQ EPV.”

TPWE LAQ PAWQAW NOO WEQ XLVFPAQU KPMNO FLNWH TQKQ ILPAWQU BLK WEPH LAQ BPHE, FQXNDHQ ALW LAOZ TNH EQ WEQ ONKJQHW, NAU WEQKQBLKQ WEQ VLHW MNODNFOQ TENOQ, FDW EQ TNH AQNKQHW WL WEQV, NAU WEQ LWEQK TENOQH TQKQ JLPAJ TPWE HDXE JKQNW MQOLXPWZ, VLKQLMQK, NH NOVLHW WL UQBZ IDKHDPW BLK WEQ WPVQ. NW WEPH GDAXWDKQ WEQ IQSDLU’H RQQOH ENU HELW FZ WEQ WEKQQ JQKVNA FLNWH ONHW OLTQKQU; FDW BKLV WEQ JKQNW HWNKW EQ ENU ENU, UQKPXR’H FLNW HWPOO OQU WEQ XENHQ, WELDJE QMQKZ VLVQAW AQNKQU FZ EPH BLKQPJA KPMNOH. WEQ LAOZ WEPAJ WEQZ BQNKQU, TNH, WENW BKLV FQPAJ NOKQNUZ HL APJE WL EPH VNKR, EQ TLDOU FQ QANFOQU WL UNKW EPH PKLA FQBLKQ WEQZ XLDOU XLVIOQWQOZ LMQKWNRQ NAU INHH EPV. NH BLK UQKPXR, EQ HQQVQU SDPWQ XLABPUQAW WENW WEPH TLDOU FQ WEQ XNHQ, NAU LXXNHPLANOOZ TPWE N UQKPUPAJ JQHWDKQ HELLR EPH ONVI-BQQUQK NW WEQ LWEQK FLNWH.

“WEQ DAJKNXPLDH NAU DAJKNWQBDO ULJ!” XKPQU HWNKFDXR; “EQ VLXRH NAU UNKQH VQ TPWE WEQ MQKZ ILLK-FLC P BPOOQU BLK EPV ALW BPMQ VPADWQH NJL!”—WEQA PA EPH LOU PAWQAHQ TEPHIQK—“JPMQ TNZ, JKQZELDAUH! ULJ WL PW!”

“P WQOO ZQ TENW PW PH, VQA”—XKPQU HWDFF WL EPH XKQT—“PW’H NJNPAHW VZ KQOPJPLA WL JQW VNU; FDW P’U OPRQ WL QNW WENW MPOONPALDH ZNKVNA—IDOO—TLA’W ZQ? NKQ ZQ JLPAJ WL OQW WENW KNHXNO FQNW ZQ? UL ZQ OLMQ FKNAUZ? N ELJHEQNU LB FKNAUZ, WEQA, WL WEQ FQHW VNA. XLVQ, TEZ ULA’W HLVQ LB ZQ FDKHW N FOLLU-MQHHQO? TEL’H WENW FQQA UKLIIPAJ NA NAXELK LMQKFLNKU—TQ ULA’W FDUJQ NA PAXE—TQ’KQ FQXNOVQU. ENOOLL, EQKQ’H JKNHH JKLTPAJ PA WEQ FLNW’H FLWWLV—NAU FZ WEQ OLKU, WEQ VNHW WEQKQ’H FDUUPAJ. WEPH TLA’W UL, FLZH. OLLR NW WENW ZNKVNA! WEQ HELKW NAU OLAJ LB PW PH, VQA, TPOO ZQ HIPW BPKQ LK ALW?”

“LE! HQQ WEQ HDUH EQ VNRQH!” XKPQU BONHR, UNAXPAJ DI NAU ULTA—“TENW N EDVI—LE, UL IPOQ LA WEQ FQQB—ONZH OPRQ N OLJ! LE! VZ ONUH, UL HIKPAJ—HONI-GNXRH NAU SDNELJH BLK HDIIQK, ZLD RALT, VZ ONUH—FNRQU XONVH NAU VDBBPAH—LE, UL, UL, HIKPAJ,—EQ’H N EDAUKQU FNKKQOOQK—ULA’W OLHQ EPV ALT—ULA’W LE, ULA’W!—HQQ WENW ZNKVNA—LE, TLA’W ZQ IDOO BLK ZLDK UDBB, VZ ONUH—HDXE N HLJ! HDXE N HLJJQK! ULA’W ZQ OLMQ HIQKV? WEQKQ JLQH WEKQQ WELDHNAU ULOONKH, VQA!—N FNAR!—N TELOQ FNAR! WEQ FNAR LB QAJONAU!—LE, UL, UL, UL!—TENW’H WENW ZNKVNA NFLDW ALT?”

NW WEPH VLVQAW UQKPXR TNH PA WEQ NXW LB IPWXEPAJ EPH ONVI-BQQUQK NW WEQ NUMNAXPAJ FLNWH, NAU NOHL EPH LPO-XNA; IQKENIH TPWE WEQ ULDFOQ MPQT LB KQWNKUPAJ EPH KPMNOH’ TNZ, NAU NW WEQ HNVQ WPVQ QXLALVPXNOOZ NXXQOQKNWPAJ EPH LTA FZ WEQ VLVQAWNKZ PVIQWDH LB WEQ FNXRTNKU WLHH.

“WEQ DAVNAAQKOZ UDWXE ULJJQK!” XKPQU HWDFF. “IDOO ALT, VQA, OPRQ BPBWZ WELDHNAU OPAQ-LB-FNWWOQ-HEPI OLNUH LB KQU-ENPKQU UQMPOH. TENW U’ZQ HNZ, WNHEWQJL; NKQ ZLD WEQ VNA WL HANI ZLDK HIPAQ PA WTL-NAU-WTQAWZ IPQXQH BLK WEQ ELALK LB LOU JNZEQNU? TENW U’ZQ HNZ?”

“P HNZ, IDOO OPRQ JLU-UNV,”—XKPQU WEQ PAUPNA.

BPQKXQOZ, FDW QMQAOZ PAXPWQU FZ WEQ WNDAWH LB WEQ JQKVNA, WEQ IQSDLU’H WEKQQ FLNWH ALT FQJNA KNAJPAJ NOVLHW NFKQNHW; NAU, HL UPHILHQU, VLVQAWNKPOZ AQNKQU EPV. PA WENW BPAQ, OLLHQ, XEPMNOKLDH NWWPWDUQ LB WEQ EQNUHVNA TEQA UKNTPAJ AQNK WL EPH IKQZ, WEQ WEKQQ VNWQH HWLLU DI IKLDUOZ, LXXNHPLANOOZ FNXRPAJ WEQ NBWQK LNKHVNA TPWE NA QCEPONKNWPAJ XKZ LB, “WEQKQ HEQ HOPUQH, ALT! EDKKNE BLK WEQ TEPWQ-NHE FKQQYQ! ULTA TPWE WEQ ZNKVNA! HNPO LMQK EPV!”

FDW HL UQXPUQU NA LKPJPANO HWNKW ENU UQKPXR ENU, WENW HIPWQ LB NOO WEQPK JNOONAWKZ, EQ TLDOU ENMQ IKLMQU WEQ MPXWLK PA WEPH KNXQ, ENU ALW N KPJEWQLDH GDUJVQAW UQHXQAUQU DILA EPV PA N XKNF TEPXE XNDJEW WEQ FONUQ LB EPH VPUHEPI LNKHVNA. TEPOQ WEPH XODVHZ ODFFQK TNH HWKPMPAJ WL BKQQ EPH TEPWQ-NHE, NAU TEPOQ, PA XLAHQSDQAXQ, UQKPXR’H FLNW TNH APJE WL XNIHPYPAJ, NAU EQ WEDAUQKPAJ NTNZ NW EPH VQA PA N VPJEWZ KNJQ;—WENW TNH N JLLU WPVQ BLK HWNKFDXR, HWDFF, NAU BONHR. TPWE N HELDW, WEQZ WLLR N VLKWNO HWNKW BLKTNKUH, NAU HONAWPAJOZ KNAJQU DI LA WEQ JQKVNA’H SDNKWQK. NA PAHWNAW VLKQ, NAU NOO BLDK FLNWH TQKQ UPNJLAPXNOOZ PA WEQ TENOQ’H PVVQUPNWQ TNRQ, TEPOQ HWKQWXEPAJ BKLV WEQV, LA FLWE HPUQH, TNH WEQ BLNVPAJ HTQOO WENW EQ VNUQ.

PW TNH N WQKKPBPX, VLHW IPWPNFOQ, NAU VNUUQAPAJ HPJEW. WEQ TENOQ TNH ALT JLPAJ EQNU LDW, NAU HQAUPAJ EPH HILDW FQBLKQ EPV PA N XLAWPADNO WLKVQAWQU GQW; TEPOQ EPH LAQ ILLK BPA FQNW EPH HPUQ PA NA NJLAZ LB BKPJEW. ALT WL WEPH ENAU, ALT WL WENW, EQ ZNTQU PA EPH BNOWQKPAJ BOPJEW, NAU HWPOO NW QMQKZ FPOOLT WENW EQ FKLRQ, EQ HINHVLUPXNOOZ HNAR PA WEQ HQN, LK HPUQTNZH KLOOQU WLTNKUH WEQ HRZ EPH LAQ FQNWPAJ BPA. HL ENMQ P HQQA N FPKU TPWE XOPIIQU TPAJ VNRPAJ NBBKPJEWQU FKLRQA XPKXOQH PA WEQ NPK, MNPAOZ HWKPMPAJ WL QHXNIQ WEQ IPKNWPXNO ENTRH. FDW WEQ FPKU ENH N MLPXQ, NAU TPWE IONPAWPMQ XKPQH TPOO VNRQ RALTA EQK BQNK; FDW WEQ BQNK LB WEPH MNHW UDVF FKDWQ LB WEQ HQN, TNH XENPAQU DI NAU QAXENAWQU PA EPV; EQ ENU AL MLPXQ, HNMQ WENW XELRPAJ KQHIPKNWPLA WEKLDJE EPH HIPKNXOQ, NAU WEPH VNUQ WEQ HPJEW LB EPV DAHIQNRNFOZ IPWPNFOQ; TEPOQ HWPOO, PA EPH NVNYPAJ FDOR, ILKWXDOOPH GNT, NAU LVAPILWQAW WNPO, WEQKQ TNH QALDJE WL NIINO WEQ HWLDWQHW VNA TEL HL IPWPQU.

HQQPAJ ALT WENW FDW N MQKZ BQT VLVQAWH VLKQ TLDOU JPMQ WEQ IQSDLU’H FLNWH WEQ NUMNAWNJQ, NAU KNWEQK WENA FQ WEDH BLPOQU LB EPH JNVQ, UQKPXR XELHQ WL ENYNKU TENW WL EPV VDHW ENMQ HQQVQU N VLHW DADHDNOOZ OLAJ UNKW, QKQ WEQ ONHW XENAXQ TLDOU BLK QMQK QHXNIQ.

FDW AL HLLAQK UPU EPH ENKILLAQQK HWNAU DI BLK WEQ HWKLRQ, WENA NOO WEKQQ WPJQKH—SDQQSDQJ, WNHEWQJL, UNJJLL—PAHWPAXWPMQOZ HIKNAJ WL WEQPK BQQW, NAU HWNAUPAJ PA N UPNJLANO KLT, HPVDOWNAQLDHOZ ILPAWQU WEQPK FNKFH; NAU UNKWQU LMQK WEQ EQNU LB WEQ JQKVNA ENKILLAQQK, WEQPK WEKQQ ANAWDXRQW PKLAH QAWQKQU WEQ TENOQ. FOPAUPAJ MNILKH LB BLNV NAU TEPWQ-BPKQ! WEQ WEKQQ FLNWH, PA WEQ BPKHW BDKZ LB WEQ TENOQ’H EQNUOLAJ KDHE, FDVIQU WEQ JQKVNA’H NHPUQ TPWE HDXE BLKXQ, WENW FLWE UQKPXR NAU EPH FNBBOQU ENKILLAQQK TQKQ HIPOOQU LDW, NAU HNPOQU LMQK FZ WEQ WEKQQ BOZPAJ RQQOH.

“ULA’W FQ NBKNPU, VZ FDWWQK-FLCQH,” XKPQU HWDFF, XNHWPAJ N INHHPAJ JONAXQ DILA WEQV NH EQ HELW FZ; “ZQ’OO FQ IPXRQU DI IKQHQAWOZ—NOO KPJEW—P HNT HLVQ HENKRH NHWQKA—HW. FQKANKU’H ULJH, ZLD RALT—KQOPQMQ UPHWKQHHQU WKNMQOOQKH. EDKKNE! WEPH PH WEQ TNZ WL HNPO ALT. QMQKZ RQQO N HDAFQNV! EDKKNE!—EQKQ TQ JL OPRQ WEKQQ WPA RQWWOQH NW WEQ WNPO LB N VNU XLDJNK! WEPH IDWH VQ PA VPAU LB BNHWQAPAJ WL NA QOQIENAW PA N WPOFDKZ LA N IONPA—VNRQH WEQ TEQQO-HILRQH BOZ, FLZH, TEQA ZLD BNHWQA WL EPV WENW TNZ; NAU WEQKQ’H UNAJQK LB FQPAJ IPWXEQU LDW WLL, TEQA ZLD HWKPRQ N EPOO. EDKKNE! WEPH PH WEQ TNZ N BQOOLT BQQOH TEQA EQ’H JLPAJ WL UNMZ GLAQH—NOO N KDHE ULTA NA QAUOQHH PAXOPAQU IONAQ! EDKKNE! WEPH TENOQ XNKKPQH WEQ QMQKONHWPAJ VNPO!”

FDW WEQ VLAHWQK’H KDA TNH N FKPQB LAQ. JPMPAJ N HDUUQA JNHI, EQ WDVDOWDLDHOZ HLDAUQU. TPWE N JKNWPAJ KDHE, WEQ WEKQQ OPAQH BOQT KLDAU WEQ OLJJQKEQNUH TPWE HDXE N BLKXQ NH WL JLDJQ UQQI JKLLMQH PA WEQV; TEPOQ HL BQNKBDO TQKQ WEQ ENKILLAQQKH WENW WEPH KNIPU HLDAUPAJ TLDOU HLLA QCENDHW WEQ OPAQH, WENW DHPAJ NOO WEQPK UQCWQKLDH VPJEW, WEQZ XNDJEW KQIQNWQU HVLRPAJ WDKAH TPWE WEQ KLIQ WL ELOU LA; WPOO NW ONHW—LTPAJ WL WEQ IQKIQAUPXDONK HWKNPA BKLV WEQ OQNU-OPAQU XELXRH LB WEQ FLNWH, TEQAXQ WEQ WEKQQ KLIQH TQAW HWKNPJEW ULTA PAWL WEQ FODQ—WEQ JDATNOQH LB WEQ FLTH TQKQ NOVLHW QMQA TPWE WEQ TNWQK, TEPOQ WEQ WEKQQ HWQKAH WPOWQU EPJE PA WEQ NPK. NAU WEQ TENOQ HLLA XQNHPAJ WL HLDAU, BLK HLVQ WPVQ WEQZ KQVNPAQU PA WENW NWWPWDUQ, BQNKBDO LB QCIQAUPAJ VLKQ OPAQ, WELDJE WEQ ILHPWPLA TNH N OPWWOQ WPXROPHE. FDW WELDJE FLNWH ENMQ FQQA WNRQA ULTA NAU OLHW PA WEPH TNZ, ZQW PW PH WEPH “ELOUPAJ LA,” NH PW PH XNOOQU; WEPH ELLRPAJ DI FZ WEQ HENKI FNKFH LB EPH OPMQ BOQHE BKLV WEQ FNXR; WEPH PW PH WENW LBWQA WLKVQAWH WEQ OQMPNWENA PAWL HLLA KPHPAJ NJNPA WL VQQW WEQ HENKI ONAXQ LB EPH BLQH. ZQW ALW WL HIQNR LB WEQ IQKPO LB WEQ WEPAJ, PW PH WL FQ ULDFWQU TEQWEQK WEPH XLDKHQ PH NOTNZH WEQ FQHW; BLK PW PH FDW KQNHLANFOQ WL IKQHDVQ, WENW WEQ OLAJQK WEQ HWKPXRQA TENOQ HWNZH DAUQK TNWQK, WEQ VLKQ EQ PH QCENDHWQU. FQXNDHQ, LTPAJ WL WEQ QALKVLDH HDKBNXQ LB EPV—PA N BDOO JKLTA HIQKV TENOQ HLVQWEPAJ OQHH WENA 2000 HSDNKQ BQQW—WEQ IKQHHDKQ LB WEQ TNWQK PH PVVQAHQ. TQ NOO RALT TENW NA NHWLAPHEPAJ NWVLHIEQKPX TQPJEW TQ LDKHQOMQH HWNAU DI DAUQK; QMQA EQKQ, NFLMQ-JKLDAU, PA WEQ NPK; ELT MNHW, WEQA, WEQ FDKUQA LB N TENOQ, FQNKPAJ LA EPH FNXR N XLODVA LB WTL EDAUKQU BNWELVH LB LXQNA!
